```dafny
ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}
```

    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {

    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}

  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {

    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDe...

{

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {

    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}

{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}
</DAFNY

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result

  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {

    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    // From invariant: init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    // Since SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed,
    // we get init - absorbed >= 0, i.e., init >= absorbed

    // the invariant ensures the pile never goes negative after minK),
    // we have FinalPileSize(s, init) >= absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) + 0
    // = absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) = result
    // We can argue more directly:
    assert FinalPileSize(s, init) == init + SumDeltas(s);
    assert init >= absorbed;
    // We know result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i]) at the end, where i == |s|
    // So result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s)
    assert result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s);
    // Therefore FinalPileSize(s, init) - result == init - absorbed >= 0
    assert FinalPileSize(s, init) - result == init - absorbed;
    assert init - absorbed >= 0;
    assert FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result;
  }

  init + SumDeltas(s)

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i

    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }

  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}

// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

  decreases |s|
{

  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]])
    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}

    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;

--- LLM RESPONSE (652 tokens, 6.31s) ---
<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}
</DAFNY

  init + SumDeltas(s)

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{

  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }

{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {

    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}
</DAFNY

  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])

// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.

{

  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0

{

ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {

    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    // From the invariant: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == 0
    assert SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed;
    // For any valid init, at step minK the pile size must be non‑negative
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    // Thus init >= absorbed
    assert init >= absorbed;
    // Consequently FinalPileSize(s, init) = init + SumDeltas(s)
    //                    >= absorbed + SumDeltas(s)
    //                    = result
    assert FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result;
  }
}

  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}
</DAFNY

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
